<h3 data-start="219" data-end="262"> Act I  The City That Never Sweeps</h3>
<ul data-start="263" data-end="698">
<li data-start="263" data-end="468">
<p data-start="265" data-end="468"><strong data-start="265" data-end="285">Opening Montage:</strong> New Yorks dawn. The left-two (rule-followers) clock in precisely at 5:59 a.m.; the right-two (whimsical duo) roll up late on a tandem bike, coffee in hand, waving to street vendors.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="469" data-end="607">
<p data-start="471" data-end="607"><strong data-start="471" data-end="493">Inciting Incident:</strong> Their route gets merged due to budget cuts, forcing all four to share one trucknicknamed <em data-start="584" data-end="606">The Garbadge Avenger</em>.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="608" data-end="698">
<p data-start="610" data-end="698"><strong data-start="610" data-end="619">Tone:</strong> Grit-meets-glowbustling city life scored with jazzy percussion on trash cans.</p>
</li>

<h3 data-start="1393" data-end="1443"> Act III  The Cleanup That Saved the City</h3>
<ul data-start="1444" data-end="1936">
<li data-start="1444" data-end="1500">
<p data-start="1446" data-end="1500">A massive heatwave or blackout hits; garbage piles up.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1501" data-end="1815">
<p data-start="1503" data-end="1583">The rule-followers planning and the whimsical duos improvisation finally fuse:</p>
<ul data-start="1586" data-end="1815">
<li data-start="1586" data-end="1625">
<p data-start="1588" data-end="1625"><strong data-start="1588" data-end="1625">One maps efficient pickup routes.</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1628" data-end="1673">
<p data-start="1630" data-end="1673"><strong data-start="1630" data-end="1673">One rigs the truck to run on bio-waste.</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1676" data-end="1747">
<p data-start="1678" data-end="1747"><strong data-start="1678" data-end="1747">One mobilizes kids from the book fair as Page-Turner Recyclers.</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1750" data-end="1815">
<p data-start="1752" data-end="1815"><strong data-start="1752" data-end="1815">One gives an impromptu street speech about dignity in work.</strong></p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="1816" data-end="1936">
<p data-start="1818" data-end="1936">The city pulls together  streets clean, gardens bloom, and the mayor renames their depot <em data-start="1908" data-end="1936">The Peoples Department.</em></p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 data-start="1943" data-end="1963"> Themes &amp; Vibe</h3>
<ul data-start="1964" data-end="2177">
<li data-start="1964" data-end="2036">
<p data-start="1966" data-end="2036"><em data-start="1966" data-end="1991">Mutual Aid Over Metrics</em>  neighbors helping neighbors, no hierarchy.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2037" data-end="2118">
<p data-start="2039" data-end="2118"><em data-start="2039" data-end="2066">Eco-Anarcho Wholesomeness</em>  direct action through compost, murals, and music.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2119" data-end="2177">
<p data-start="2121" data-end="2177"><em data-start="2121" data-end="2143">Reclaiming the Badge</em>  symbol of pride, not authority.</p>
</li>
</ul>
